*template.Template\n27\t}\n28\t\n29\t// New creates a new Dashboard.\n30\tfunc New(b backend.Backend, bucket string, m *metrics.Metrics) *Dashboard {\n31\t\td := &Dashboard{\n32\t\t\tbackend: KeyRotateStatusHandler returns the current key rotation status.\n41\t// This polls the rotation state file from B2 for progress information.\n42\tfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateStatusHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n43\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n44\t\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n45\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n46\t\t\t\treturn\n47\t\t\t}\n48\t\n49\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 10*time.Second)\n50\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n51\t\n52\t\t\t// Try to read the rotation state file\n53\t\t\tstatePath := \".armor/rotation-state.json\"\n54\t\t\treader, _, err := d.backend.GetDirect(ctx, d.bucket, statePath)\n55\t\t\tif err != nil {\n56\t\t\t\t// No rotation state file means no rotation in progress\n57\t\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n58\t\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n59\t\t\t\t\t\"status\": \"none\",\n60\t\t\t\t\t\"message\": \"No rotation in progress\",\n61\t\t\t\t})\n62\t\t\t\treturn\n63\t\t\t}\n64\t\t\tdefer reader.Close()\n65\t\n66\t\t\tdata, err := io.ReadAll(reader)\n67\t\t\tif err != nil {\n68\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read state: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n69\t\t\t\treturn\n70\t\t\t}\n71\t\n72\t\t\t// Return the raw state file content\n73\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n74\t\t\tw.Write(data)\n75\t\t}\n76\t}\n77\t\n78\t// Handler returns the main dashboard handler.\n79\tfunc (d *Dashboard) Handler() http.HandlerFunc {\n80\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n81\t\t\t// Get prefix from query\n82\t\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n83\t\n84\t\t\t// List objects\n85\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n86\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n87\t\n88\t\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"/\", \"\", 1000)\n89\t\t\tif err != nil {\n90\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n91\t\t\t\treturn\n92\t\t\t}\n93\t\n94\t\t\t// Build page data\n95\t\t\tdata := d.buildPageData(result, prefix)\n96\t\n97\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/html; charset=utf-8\")\n98\t\t\tif err := d.template.Execute(w, data); err != nil {\n99\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Template error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n100\t\t\t\treturn\n101\t\t\t}\n102\t\t}\n103\t}\n104\t\n105\t// ObjectInfo represents an object in the dashboard.\n106\ttype ObjectInfo struct {\n107\t\tKey            string\n108\t\tSize           int64\n109\t\tPlaintextSize  int64\n110\t\tLastModified   string\n111\t\tIsARMOR        bool\n112\t\tContentType    string\n113\t\tETag           string\n114\t\tKeyID          string\n115\t\tBlockSize      int\n116\t\tIsFolder       bool\n117\t\tPlaintextSizeH string\n118\t}\n119\t\n120\t// PageData holds data for the dashboard template.\n121\ttype PageData struct {\n122\t\tBucket       string\n123\t\tPrefix       string\n124\t\tObjects      []ObjectInfo\n125\t\tCacheHits    string\n126\t\tCacheMisses  string\n127\t\tCacheHitRate string\n128\t\tUptime       string\n129\t\tRequests     string\n130\t\tBytesUp      string\n131\t\tBytesDown    string\n132\t\tCanaryStatus string\n133\t\tBreadcrumbs  []Breadcrumb\n134\t}\n135\t\n136\t// Breadcrumb represents a navigation breadcrumb.\n137\ttype Breadcrumb struct {\n138\t\tName string\n139\t\tPath string\n140\t}\n141\t\n142\tfunc (d *Dashboard) buildPageData(result *backend.ListResult, prefix string) PageData {\n143\t\tobjects := make([]ObjectInfo, 0, len(result.Objects))\n144\t\n145\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n146\t\t\tinfo := ObjectInfo{\n147\t\t\t\tKey:          obj.Key,\n148\t\t\t\tSize:         obj.Size,\n149\t\t\t\tLastModified: obj.LastModified.Format(\"2006-01-02 15:04:05\"),\n150\t\t\t\tContentType:  obj.ContentType,\n151\t\t\t\tETag:         obj.ETag,\n152\t\t\t\tIsFolder:     strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\"),\n153\t\t\t}\n154\t\n155\t\t\t// Check if ARMOR-encrypted\n156\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n157\t\t\t\tinfo.IsARMOR = true\n158\t\t\t\t// Size is already plaintext size for ARMOR objects\n159\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSize = obj.Size\n160\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSizeH = formatBytes(obj.Size)\n161\t\t\t\t// Extract additional ARMOR metadata\n162\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok {\n163\t\t\t\t\tinfo.KeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n164\t\t\t\t\tinfo.BlockSize = armorMeta.BlockSize\n165\t\t\t\t}\n166\t\t\t} else {\n167\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSize = obj.Size\n168\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSizeH = formatBytes(obj.Size)\n169\t\t\t}\n170\t\n171\t\t\tobjects = append(objects, info)\n172\t\t}\n173\t\n174\t\t// Build breadcrumbs\n175\t\tbreadcrumbs := []Breadcrumb{{Name: d.bucket, Path: \"\"}}\n176\t\tif prefix != \"\" {\n177\t\t\tparts := strings.Split(strings.TrimSuffix(prefix, \"/\"), \"/\")\n178\t\t\tpath := \"\"\n179\t\t\tfor _, part := range parts {\n180\t\t\t\tif part == \"\" {\n181\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n182\t\t\t\t}\n183\t\t\t\tpath += part + \"/\"\n184\t\t\t\tbreadcrumbs = append(breadcrumbs, Breadcrumb{Name: part, Path: path})\n185\t\t\t}\n186\t\t}\n187\t\n188\t\t// Get metrics\n189\t\tcacheHits := d.metrics.CacheHitsTotal.String()\n190\t\tcacheMisses := d.metrics.CacheMissesTotal.String()\n191\t\thitRate := \"0%\"\n192\t\tif hits, misses := parseExpvarInt(cacheHits), parseExpvarInt(cacheMisses); hits+misses > 0 {\n193\t\t\trate := float64(hits) / float64(hits+misses) * 100\n194\t\t\thitRate = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f%%\", rate)\n195\t\t}\n196\t\n197\t\treturn PageData{\n198\t\t\tBucket:       d.bucket,\n199\t\t\tPrefix:       prefix,\n200\t\t\tObjects:      objects,\n201\t\t\tCacheHits:    cacheHits,\n202\t\t\tCacheMisses:  cacheMisses,\n203\t\t\tCacheHitRate: hitRate,\n204\t\t\tUptime:       formatUptime(time.Since(d.metrics.StartTime())),\n205\t\t\tRequests:     d.metrics.RequestsTotal.String(),\n206\t\t\tBytesUp:      formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesUploaded.String())),\n207\t\t\tBytesDown:    formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesDownloaded.String())),\n208\t\t\tCanaryStatus: d.metrics.CanaryLastCheckTime.String()\n215\t\tfailures := d.metrics.CanaryCheckFailures.String()\n216\t\n217\t\tif parseExpvarInt(failures) > 0 {\n218\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Unhealthy (failures: %s)\", failures)\n219\t\t}\n220\t\tif lastCheck == \"\" {\n221\t\t\treturn \"Not started\"\n222\t\t}\n223\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Healthy (last check: %s)\", lastCheck)\n224\t}\n225\t\n226\t// ObjectDetailHandler returns details for a specific object.\n227\tfunc (d *Dashboard) ObjectDetailHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n228\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n229\t\t\tkey := r.URL.Query().Get(\"key\")\n230\t\t\tif key == \"\" {\n231\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"key parameter required\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n232\t\t\t\treturn\n233\t\t\t}\n234\t\n235\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n236\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n237\t\n238\t\t\tinfo, err := http.StatusNotFound)\n241\t\t\t\treturn\n242\t\t\t}\n243\t\n244\t\t\t// Build response\n245\t\t\tdetail := map[string]interface{}{\n246\t\t\t\t\"key\":             key,\n247\t\t\t\t\"size\":            info.Size,\n248\t\t\t\t\"content_type\":    info.ContentType,\n249\t\t\t\t\"etag\":            info.ETag,\n250\t\t\t\t\"last_modified\":   info.LastModified.Format(time.RFC3339),\n251\t\t\t\t\"is_armor\":        info.IsARMOREncrypted,\n252\t\t\t}\n253\t\n254\t\t\tif info.IsARMOREncrypted {\n255\t\t\t\tarmorMeta, ok := armorMeta.PlaintextSize,\n259\t\t\t\t\t\t\"block_size\":     armorMeta.BlockSize,\n260\t\t\t\t\t\t\"key_id\":         armorMeta.KeyID,\n261\t\t\t\t\t\t\"iv\":             fmt.Sprintf(\"%x\", armorMeta.IV),\n262\t\t\t\t\t\t\"wrapped_dek\":    fmt.Sprintf(\"%x\", armorMeta.WrappedDEK),\n263\t\t\t\t\t\t\"sha256\":         armorMeta.PlaintextSHA,\n264\t\t\t\t\t}\n265\t\t\t\t}\n266\t\t\t}\n267\t\n268\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n269\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(detail)\n270\t\t}\n271\t}\n272\t\n273\t// MetricsHandler returns metrics in JSON format.\n274\tfunc (d *Dashboard) MetricsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n275\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n276\t\t\tm := d.metrics\n277\t\t\tdata := map[string]interface{}{\n278\t\t\t\t\"requests_total\": parseExpvarInt(m.CanaryCheckFailures.String()),\n291\t\t\t\t\"active_multipart\":       parseExpvarInt(m.ActiveMultipartUploads.String()),\n292\t\t\t\t\"provenance_entries\": \"application/json\")\n296\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(data)\n297\t\t}\n298\t}\n299\t\n300\t// KeyRotateHandler handles key rotation requests.\n301\t// It generates a new MEK and calls the admin API to perform rotation.\n302\tfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandler(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n303\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n304\t\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n305\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n306\t\t\t\treturn\n307\t\t\t}\n308\t\n309\t\t\t// Generate a new MEK (32 random bytes)\n310\t\t\tnewMEK := make([]byte, 32)\n311\t\t\tif _, err := rand.Read(newMEK); err != nil {\n312\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate new MEK: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n313\t\t\t\treturn\n314\t\t\t}\n315\t\n316\t\t\t// Call the admin API's rotate endpoint\n317\t\t\trotateURL := adminURL\n318\t\t\tif rotateURL == \"\" {\n319\t\t\t\trotateURL = \"http://127.0.0.1:9001/admin/key/rotate\"\n320\t\t\t}\n321\t\n322\t\t\t// Send the new MEK as hex-encoded string\n323\t\t\tmekHex := hex.EncodeToString(newMEK)\n324\t\t\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(r.Context(), http.MethodPost, rotateURL, strings.NewReader(mekHex))\n325\t\t\tif err != nil {\n326\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to create request: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n327\t\t\t\treturn\n328\t\t\t}\n329\t\t\treq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain\")\n330\t\n331\t\t\tresp, err := adminClient.Do(req)\n332\t\t\tif err != nil {\n333\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to call admin API: %v\", err), http.StatusBadGateway)\n334\t\t\t\treturn\n335\t\t\t}\n336\t\t\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n337\t\n338\t\t\t// Copy response headers and body\n339\t\t\tfor k, v := range resp.Header {\n340\t\t\t\tw.Header()[k] = v\n341\t\t\t}\n342\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(resp.StatusCode)\n343\t\t\tio.Copy(w, resp.Body)\n344\t\t}\n345\t}\n346\t\n347\t// Helper functions\n348\t\n349\tfunc parseExpvarInt(s string) int64 {\n350\t\tn, _ := strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n351\t\treturn n\n352\t}\n353\t\n354\tfunc formatBytes(n int64) string {\n355\t\tif n < 1024 {\n356\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d B\", n)\n357\t\t}\n358\t\tif n < 1024*1024 {\n359\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f KB\", float64(n)/1024)\n360\t\t}\n361\t\tif n < 1024*1024*1024 {\n362\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f MB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024))\n363\t\t}\n364\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f GB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024*1024))\n365\t}\n366\t\n367\tfunc formatUptime(d time.Duration) string {\n368\t\td = d.Round(time.Second)\n369\t\th := d / time.Hour\n370\t\td -= h * time.Hour\n371\t\tm := d / time.Minute\n372\t\td -= m * time.Minute\n373\t\ts := d / time.Second\n374\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%dh %dm %ds\", h, m, s)\n375\t}\n376\t\n377\t// The HTML template for the dashboard\n378\tconst dashboardHTML = `<!DOCTYPE html>\n379\t<html lang=\"en\">\n380\t<head>\n381\t    <meta charset=\"UTF-8\">\n382\t {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Generate a new MEK (32 random bytes)\n\t\tnewMEK := make([]byte, 32)\n\t\tif _, err := functions\n\nfunc parseExpvarInt(s string) int64 {\n\tn, _ := strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n\treturn n\n}\n\nfunc formatBytes(n int64) string {\n\tif n < 1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d B\", credential env var\n\t\t\tif envKey == \"ARMOR_AUTH_ACCESS_KEY\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tnamePart := strings.TrimPrefix(envKey, \"ARMOR_AUTH_\")\n\t\t\tnamePart = entries.\n// Format: \"bucket1:prefix1,bucket2:prefix2,bucket3:*\"\n// A bucket of \"*\" means all buckets.\n// A prefix of \"*\" or \"\" means any prefix within the bucket.\nfunc parseACL(aclStr string) ([]ACLEntry, error) {\n\tif aclStr == \"\" {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar entries []ACLEntry\n\tparts := strings.Split(aclStr, \",\")\n\n\tfor _, part := range parts {\n\t\tpart = nil, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid ACL entry %q (empty bucket)\", part)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Normalize wildcard prefix\n\t\tif prefix == \"*\" {\n\t\t\tprefix = \"\"\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tentries = append(entries, s.config.AdminListen + \"/admin/key/rotate\"\n416\t\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/admin/key/rotate\", s.dashboard.KeyRotateHandler(adminClient, adminURL))\n417\t\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/admin/key/status\", s.dashboard.KeyRotateStatusHandler())\n418\t\t}\n419\t\n420\t\treturn mux\n421\t}\n422\t\n423\t// healthz returns the health status.\n424\t// This is the liveness probe — it only checks that the process is alive.\n425\t// Backend connectivity is checked by /readyz (the readiness probe).\n426\tfunc (s *Server) healthz(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n427\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n428\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"OK\"))\n429\t}\n430\t\n431\t// readyz returns the readiness status.\n432\t// When the canary monitor is running and not disabled, its in-memory health\n433\t// state is the sole signal — no backend call is made. When the canary is\n434\t// disabled (ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true), /readyz always returns 200 and the\n435\t// liveness probe (/healthz) is the sole health guard. When the canary is not\n436\t// configured, the manifest writer's last flush is used as the health signal.\n437\tfunc (s *Server) readyz(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n438\t\t// When canary is explicitly disabled, skip all backend checks.\n439\t\tif s.canaryDisabled {\n440\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n441\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n442\t\t\treturn\n443\t\t}\n444\t\n445\t\t// Canary monitor is authoritative when running.\n446\t\tif s.canary != nil && s.canaryStarted {\n447\t\t\tif !s.canary.IsHealthy() {\n448\t\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n449\t\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - canary check failed\"))\n450\t\t\t\treturn\n451\t\t\t}\n452\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n453\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n454\t\t\treturn\n455\t\t}\n456\t\n457\t\t// Fallback: manifest writer's last successful delta flush.\n458\t\t// A flush within the last 60 seconds indicates the service is healthy.\n459\t\tconst flushThreshold = 60 * time.Second\n460\t\tif s.manifestWriter != nil {\n461\t\t\tlastFlush := s.manifestWriter.LastFlush()\n462\t\t\tif !lastFlush.IsZero() && time.Since(lastFlush) < flushThreshold {\n463\t\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n464\t\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n465\t\t\t\treturn\n466\t\t\t}\n467\t\t\t// No recent flush — report unhealthy\n468\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n469\t\t\tif lastFlush.IsZero() {\n470\t\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - manifest writer has never flushed\"))\n471\t\t\t} else {\n472\t\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(fmt.Sprintf(\"Not ready - manifest writer last flush %v ago (threshold %v)\", time.Since(lastFlush).Round(time.Second), flushThreshold)))\n473\t\t\t}\n474\t\t\treturn\n475\t\t}\n476\t\n477\t\t// Neither canary nor manifest writer available — report unhealthy.\n478\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n479\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - no health signal available\"))\n480\t}\n481\t\n482\t// verifyKey verifies the MEK is correct.\n483\tfunc (s *Server) verifyKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n484\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n485\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n486\t\t\treturn\n487\t\t}\n488\t\n489\t\tif s.canary == nil {\n490\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n491\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unknown\",\"error\":\"canary monitor not configured\"}`))\n492\t\t\treturn\n493\t\t}\n494\t\n495\t\tstatus := s.canary.GetStatus()\n496\t\tif status.DecryptVerified && status.HMACVerified {\n497\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n498\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"verified\",\"message\":\"MEK is correct\"}`))\n499\t\t\treturn\n500\t\t}\n501\t\n502\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n503\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unverified\",\"error\":\"canary check failed - MEK may be incorrect\"}`))\n504\t}\n505\t\n506\t// rotateKey rotates the MEK.\n507\tfunc (s *Server) rotateKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n508\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n509\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n510\t\t\treturn\n511\t\t}\n512\t\n513\t\t// Read the new MEK from the request body\n514\t\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)\n515\t\tif err != nil {\n516\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n517\t\t\treturn\n518\t\t}\n519\t\tdefer r.Body.Close()\n520\t\n521\t\t// The new MEK should be a 32-byte hex-encoded string (64 hex chars)\n522\t\t// or raw 32 bytes\n523\t\tvar newMEK []byte\n524\t\tif len(body) == 64 {\n525\t\t\t// Hex-encoded\n526\t\t\tnewMEK, err = hex.DecodeString(string(body))\n527\t\t\tif err != nil {\n528\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid hex-encoded MEK\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n529\t\t\t\treturn\n530\t\t\t}\n531\t\t} else if len(body) == 32 {\n532\t\t\t// Raw bytes\n533\t\t\tnewMEK = body\n534\t\t} else {\n535\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid MEK length: expected 32 bytes or 64 hex chars, got %d\", len(body)), http.StatusBadRequest)\n536\t\t\treturn\n537\t\t}\n538\t\n539\t\t// Create key rotator with the default key. Pass the manifest index so\n540\t\t// rotateObject can skip per-object HeadObject calls when the entry is cached.\n541\t\tdefaultKey := s.keyManager.DefaultKey()\n542\t\trotator := NewKeyRotator(s.backend, s.config.Bucket, defaultKey.MEK, newMEK, s.manifest)\n543\t\n544\t\t// Perform rotation\n545\t\tresult, err := rotator.Rotate(r.Context())\n546\t\tif err != nil {\n547\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n548\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n549\t\t\t\t\"status\":  \"failed\",\n550\t\t\t\t\"error\":   err.Error(),\n551\t\t\t\t\"result\":  result,\n552\t\t\t})\n553\t\t\treturn\n554\t\t}\n555\t\n556\t\t// Update the server's MEK on success\n557\t\tif result.Status == \"completed\" {\n558\t\t\tif err := s.keyManager.UpdateDefaultKey(newMEK); err != nil {\n559\t\t\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n560\t\t\t\t\t\"error\": err.Error(),\n561\t\t\t\t}).Error(\"failed to update key manager after rotation\")\n562\t\t\t}\n563\t\t\t// Clear the metadata cache since DEKs are now wrapped with new MEK\n564\t\t\ts.cache.Clear()\n565\t\t}\n566\t\n567\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n568\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n569\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(result)\n570\t}\n571\t\n572\t// exportKey exports the current MEK.\n573\tfunc (s *Server) exportKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n574\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n575\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n576\t\t\treturn\n577\t\t}\n578\t\n579\t\tif r.URL.Query().Get(\"confirm\") != \"yes\" {\n580\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Must include ?confirm=yes to export key\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n581\t\t\treturn\n582\t\t}\n583\t\n584\t\t// Export the default MEK as hex-encoded string\n585\t\tdefaultKey := s.keyManager.DefaultKey()\n586\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n587\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n588\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]string{\n589\t\t\t\"mek\":   hex.EncodeToString(defaultKey.MEK),\n590\t\t\t\"format\": \"hex\",\n591\t\t\t\"warning\": \"This key provides access to all encrypted data. wrapHandler(h http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {\n640\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n641\t\t\tstart := time.Now()\n642\t\n643\t\t\t// Track in-flight request\n644\t\t\ts.requestTracker.Start()\n645\t\t\tdefer s.requestTracker.End()\n646\t\n647\t\t\t// Log request\n648\t\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n649\t\t\t\t\"method\": 403)\n669\t\t\t\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(\"auth\", 403)\n670\t\t\t\t\treturn\n671\t\t\t\t}\n672\t\t\t\t// Check ACL for the request. 403)\n682\t\t\t\t\treturn\n683\t\t\t\t}\n684\t\t\t}\n685\t\n686\t\t\t// Use a response writer wrapper to capture status code\n687\t\t\trw := &responseWriter{ResponseWriter: w, statusCode: http.StatusOK}\n688\t\n689\t\t\th(rw, r)\n690\t\n691\t\t\t// Record metrics\n692\t\t\tduration := time.Since(start)\n693\t\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(r.Method, rw.statusCode)\n694\t\t\ts.metrics.RecordRequestDuration(r.Method, duration)\n695\t\n696\t\t\t// Log completed request\n697\t\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n698\t\t\t\t\"method\":      r.Method,\n699\t\t\t\t\"path\":        r.URL.Path,\n700\t\t\t\t\"status\":      rw.statusCode,\n701\t\t\t\t\"duration_ms\": duration.Milliseconds(),\n702\t\t\t}).Info(\"request completed\")\n703\t\t}\n704\t}\n705\t\n706\t// responseWriter wraps http.ResponseWriter to capture the status code.\n707\ttype responseWriter struct {\n708\t\thttp.ResponseWriter\n709\t\tstatusCode code\n715\t\trw.ResponseWriter.WriteHeader(code)\n716\t}\n717\t\n718\t// isPublicPath checks if a path is public (no auth required).\n719\tfunc (s *Server) isPublicPath(path string) bool {\n720\t\treturn path == \"/healthz\" || path == \"/readyz\"\n721\t}\n722\t\n723\t// verifyAuthAndGetCredential validates AWS SigV4 authentication and returns the credential.\n724\tfunc (s *Server) verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r *http.Request) (*config.Credential, error) {\n725\t\t// Create auth with all credentials\n726\t\tauth := NewSigV4AuthWithCredentials(s.config.Credentials, s.config.B2Region)\n727\t\n728\t\t// Check for query-based auth (presigned URLs)\n729\t\tif r.URL.Query().Get(\"X-Amz-Credential\") != \"\" {\n730\t\t\treturn \"/\")\n750\t\n751\t\t// Check for virtual-hosted-style (bucket in host)\n752\t\t// For path-style: /bucket/key\n753\t\tparts := strings.SplitN(path, \"/\", 2)\n754\t\tif len(parts) >= 1 {\n755\t\t\tbucket = parts[0]\n756\t\t}\n757\t\tif len(parts) >= 2 {\n758\t\t\tkey = parts[1]\n759\t\t\t// URL decode the key (DuckDB httpfs encodes special chars like = as %3D)\n760\t\t\tif decoded, pre-signed URL token.\n888\t// GET /share/<token>\n889\tfunc (s *Server) handleShare(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n890\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n891\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n892\t\t\treturn\n893\t\t}\n894\t\n895\t\t// Extract token from path\n896\t\ttokenStr := presign.ParseTokenFromPath(r.URL.Path)\n897\t\tif tokenStr == \"\" request tracking\n\tmetrics       *metrics.Metrics\n\trequestTracker *metrics.RequestTracker\n\tlogger        *logging.Logger\n}\n\n// New creates a new ARMOR server.\nfunc New(cfg *config.Config) (*Server, error) {\n\t// Create B2 backend\n\tb2Backend, err := backend.NewB2Backend(context.Background(), backend.B2Config{\n\t\tRegion:      cfg.B2Region,\n\t\tEndpoint:    cfg.B2Endpoint,\n\t\tAccessKeyID: cfg.B2AccessKeyID,\n\t\tSecretKey:   cfg.B2SecretAccessKey,\n\t\tCFDomain:    cfg.CFDomain,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create B2 backend: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create metadata cache\n\tcache := backend.NewMetadataCache(cfg.CacheMaxEntries, cfg.CacheTTL)\n\n\t// Create footer cache (for Parquet footer pinning)\n\tfooterCache := backend.NewFooterCache(cfg.CacheMaxEntries, cfg.CacheTTL)\n\n\t// Create list cache (nil when TTL is 0, meaning disabled)\n\tvar listCache *backend.ListCache\n\tif cfg.ListCacheTTL > 0 {\n\t\tlistCache = backend.NewListCache(cfg.ListCacheMaxEntries, cfg.ListCacheTTL)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create key manager\n\t// Convert config.KeyRoutes to keymanager.Route format\n\tvar routes []keymanager.Route\n\tfor _, r := range cfg.KeyRoutes {\n\t\troutes = append(routes, keymanager.Route{\n\t\t\tPrefix:  r.Prefix,\n\t\t\tKeyName: r.KeyName,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\tkeyMgr, err := keymanager.New(cfg.MEK, cfg.NamedKeys, routes)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create key manager: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create canary monitor\n\tcanaryMonitor := canary.NewMonitor(canary.Config{\n\t\tBackend:    b2Backend,\n\t\tBucket:     cfg.Bucket,\n\t\tMEK:        cfg.MEK,\n\t\tBlockSize:  cfg.BlockSize,\n\t\tInstanceID: cfg.WriterID,\n\t\tInterval:   5 * time.Minute,\n\t\tCanarySize: 1024,\n\t\tMaxRetries: 3,\n\t\tRetryDelay: 10 * time.Second,\n\t})\n\n\t// Create provenance manager\n\tprovenanceMgr := provenance.NewManager(b2Backend, cfg.Bucket, cfg.WriterID)\n\n\t// Create logger\n\tlogger := logging.New(\"armor\")\n\n\t// Create presign signer\n\tpresigner := presign.NewSigner(cfg.PresignSecret, cfg.PresignBaseURL)\n\n\t// Create B2 keys client (for B2 native API key management)\n\t// Uses the same B2 credentials as the S3 backend\n\tvar b2keysClient *b2keys.Client\n\tif cfg.Bucket != \"\" {\n\t\t// Bucket-scoped configuration: application key is restricted to a single bucket\n\t\t// and cannot call account-level B2 API endpoints (like b2_authorize_account).\n\t\t// Key management is unavailable in this mode, which is expected and intentional.\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"B2 key management disabled (application key is bucket-scoped)\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// No bucket restriction: attempt to create B2 keys client for account-level operations\n\t\t// Extract account ID from the key ID (B2 key IDs are in format accountIdKeyId)\n\t\t// The account ID is the first 12 characters\n\t\taccountID := cfg.B2AccessKeyID\n\t\tif len(accountID) > 12 {\n\t\t\taccountID = accountID[:12]\n\t\t}\n\t\tb2keysClient, err = b2keys.NewClient(context.Background(), accountID, cfg.B2SecretAccessKey)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"error\": err.Error(),\n\t\t\t}).Warn(\"Failed to create B2 keys client - key management disabled\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Create dashboard\n\tdash := dashboard.New(b2Backend, cfg.Bucket, metrics.DefaultMetrics)\n\n\t// Load manifest index from B2 (startup load).\n\t// The manifest is a performance optimisation — errors are logged as warnings\n\t// and do not prevent startup.\n\tvar manifestIdx *manifest.Index\n\tif cfg.ManifestEnabled {\n\t\tmanifestIdx = manifest.New()\n\t\t// ListRaw bypasses the .armor/ filter so manifest keys are discoverable.\n\t\tlister := func(ctx context.Context, prefix, token string) ([]string, string, error) {\n\t\t\tresult, lerr := b2Backend.ListRaw(ctx, cfg.Bucket, prefix, \"\", token, 1000)\n\t\t\tif lerr != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, \"\", lerr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeys := make([]string, len(result.Objects))\n\t\t\tfor i, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\t\tkeys[i] = obj.Key\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn keys, result.NextToken, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Fetch snapshot and delta blobs via Cloudflare for free egress and edge\n\t\t// caching. Fall back to direct B2 if no Cloudflare domain is configured.\n\t\tfetcher := func(ctx context.Context, key string) ([]byte, error) {\n\t\t\tvar body io.ReadCloser\n\t\t\tvar ferr error\n\t\t\tif cfg.CFDomain != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tbody, _, ferr = b2Backend.Get(ctx, cfg.Bucket, key)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tbody, _, ferr = b2Backend.GetDirect(ctx, cfg.Bucket, key)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif ferr != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, ferr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefer body.Close()\n\t\t\treturn io.ReadAll(body)\n\t\t}\n\t\tloadStart := time.Now()\n\t\tif loadErr := manifest.Load(context.Background(), manifestIdx, cfg.ManifestPrefix, cfg.WriterID, lister, fetcher); loadErr != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"error\": loadErr.Error(),\n\t\t\t}).Warn(\"manifest startup load failed — continuing with empty manifest index\")\n\t\t\tmanifestIdx = manifest.New() // reset to empty on error\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlogger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"entries\":  manifestIdx.Len(),\n\t\t\t\t\"seq\":      manifestIdx.Seq(),\n\t\t\t\t\"duration\": time.Since(loadStart).String(),\n\t\t\t}).Info(\"manifest index loaded\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Create and start the manifest writer (async delta persistence to B2).\n\t// Uploads go direct to B2 (free ingress); no Cloudflare path needed here.\n\tvar manifestWriter *manifest.Writer\n\tvar manifestCompactor *manifest.Compactor\n\tif manifestIdx != nil {\n\t\tuploader := func(ctx context.Context, key string, data []byte) error {\n\t\t\treturn b2Backend.Put(ctx, cfg.Bucket, key, bytes.NewReader(data), int64(len(data)), nil)\n\t\t}\n\t\tmanifestWriter = manifest.NewWriter(manifestIdx, cfg.ManifestPrefix, cfg.WriterID, uploader, 0)\n\n\t\t// Create compactor that lists and batch-deletes via the B2 backend.\n\t\tlisterForCompactor := func(ctx context.Context, prefix, token string) ([]string, string, error) {\n\t\t\tresult, lerr := b2Backend.ListRaw(ctx, cfg.Bucket, prefix, \"\", token, 1000)\n\t\t\tif lerr != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, \"\", lerr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeys := make([]string, len(result.Objects))\n\t\t\tfor i, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\t\tkeys[i] = obj.Key\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn keys, result.NextToken, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tdeleter := func(ctx context.Context, keys []string) error {\n\t\t\treturn b2Backend.DeleteObjects(ctx, cfg.Bucket, keys)\n\t\t}\n\t\tcompactionInterval := time.Duration(cfg.ManifestCompactionInterval) * time.Second\n\t\tmanifestCompactor = manifest.NewCompactor(\n\t\t\tmanifestIdx,\n\t\t\tcfg.ManifestPrefix,\n\t\t\tcfg.WriterID,\n\t\t\tuploader,\n\t\t\tlisterForCompactor,\n\t\t\tdeleter,\n\t\t\tcompactionInterval,\n\t\t\tcfg.ManifestCompactionThreshold,\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// Wire writer → compactor: after each delta flush, notify compactor.\n\t\tmanifestWriter.SetOnFlush(manifestCompactor.NotifyDelta)\n\n\t\tmanifestWriter.Start(context.Background())\n\t\tmanifestCompactor.Start(context.Background())\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"manifest writer and compactor started\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn &Server{\n\t\tconfig:         cfg,\n\t\tbackend:        b2Backend,\n\t\tcache:          cache,\n\t\tfooterCache:    footerCache,\n\t\tlistCache:      listCache,\n\t\tkeyManager:     keyMgr,\n\t\tcanary:         canaryMonitor,\n\t\tcanaryDisabled: cfg.CanaryDisabled,\n\t\tprovenance:     provenanceMgr,\n\t\tpresigner:      presigner,\n\t\tb2keys:         b2keysClient,\n\t\tdashboard:      dash,\n\t\tmanifest:          manifestIdx,\n\t\tmanifestWriter:    manifestWriter,\n\t\tmanifestCompactor: manifestCompactor,\n\t\tmetrics:        metrics.DefaultMetrics,\n\t\trequestTracker: metrics.DefaultRequestTracker,\n\t\tlogger:         logger,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// manifestRecorder implements handlers.ManifestRecorder. It updates the\n// in-memory index synchronously (so subsequent HeadObject calls see the new\n// state immediately) and enqueues the op for async B2 delta persistence.\ntype manifestRecorder struct {\n\tidx    *manifest.Index\n\twriter *manifest.Writer\n}\n\nfunc (m *manifestRecorder) RecordPut(bucket, key string, size int64, sha256Hex string, iv, wrappedDEK []byte, blockSize int, contentType, etag string) {\n\tentry := &manifest.Entry{\n\t\tPlaintextSize:   size,\n\t\tPlaintextSHA256: sha256Hex,\n\t\tIV:              iv,\n\t\tWrappedDEK:      wrappedDEK,\n\t\tBlockSize:       blockSize,\n\t\tContentType:     contentType,\n\t\tETag:            etag,\n\t\tLastModified:    time.Now().UTC(),\n\t}\n\tm.idx.Put(bucket, key, entry)\n\tm.writer.EnqueuePut(bucket, key, entry)\n}\n\nfunc (m *manifestRecorder) RecordDelete(bucket, key string) {\n\tm.idx.Delete(bucket, key)\n\tm.writer.EnqueueDelete(bucket, key)\n}\n\nfunc (m *manifestRecorder) Lookup(bucket, key string) (*handlers.ManifestEntry, bool) {\n\tentry, ok := m.idx.Get(bucket, key)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, false\n\t}\n\treturn &handlers.ManifestEntry{\n\t\tPlaintextSize: entry.PlaintextSize,\n\t\tContentType:   entry.ContentType,\n\t\tETag:          entry.ETag,\n\t\tLastModified:  entry.LastModified,\n\t\tIV:            entry.IV,\n\t\tWrappedDEK:    entry.WrappedDEK,\n\t\tBlockSize:     entry.BlockSize,\n\t}, true\n}\n\n// StopManifestWriter flushes any pending manifest ops and stops the async writer.\nfunc (s *Server) StopManifestWriter() {\n\tif s.manifestWriter != nil {\n\t\ts.manifestWriter.Stop()\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"manifest writer stopped\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// StopManifestCompactor stops the background compaction goroutine.\nfunc (s *Server) StopManifestCompactor() {\n\tif s.manifestCompactor != nil {\n\t\ts.manifestCompactor.Stop()\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"manifest compactor stopped\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// StartCanary starts the canary monitor.\n// It should be called after the server is created.\n// When ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true, the monitor is not started and /readyz\n// always returns 200 regardless of B2 reachability.\nfunc (s *Server) StartCanary(ctx context.Context) {\n\tif s.canary == nil || s.canaryStarted {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif s.canaryDisabled {\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Canary monitor disabled (ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true)\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\ts.canaryStarted = true\n\ts.canary.Start(ctx)\n\ts.logger.Info(\"Canary monitor started\")\n}\n\n// StopCanary stops the canary monitor.\nfunc (s *Server) StopCanary() {\n\tif s.canary != nil && s.canaryStarted {\n\t\ts.canary.Stop()\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Canary monitor stopped\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// Handler returns the main S3 API handler.\nfunc (s *Server) Handler() http.Handler {\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\n\t// Health endpoints\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/healthz\", s.healthz)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/readyz\", s.readyz)\n\n\t// Share endpoint for pre-signed URLs (public, no auth required)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/share/\", s.handleShare)\n\n\t// S3 operations\n\th := handlers.New(s.config, s.backend, s.cache, s.footerCache, s.keyManager, s.listCache)\n\n\t// Wire up provenance if available\n\tif s.provenance != nil {\n\t\th.WithProvenance(s.provenance)\n\t}\n\n\t// Wire up manifest recorder if enabled\n\tif s.manifest != nil && s.manifestWriter != nil {\n\t\th.WithManifest(&manifestRecorder{idx: s.manifest, writer: s.manifestWriter})\n\t}\n\n\t// Bucket operations\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/\", s.wrapHandler(h.HandleRoot))\n\n\treturn mux\n}\n\n// AdminHandler returns the admin API handler.\nfunc (s *Server) AdminHandler() http.Handler {\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/healthz\", s.healthz)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/key/verify\", s.verifyKey)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/key/rotate\", s.rotateKey)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/key/export\", s.exportKey)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/armor/canary\", s.canaryHandler)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/armor/audit\", s.audit)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/presign\", s.handlePresign)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/b2/keys\", s.handleB2Keys)           // GET=List, POST=Create\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/b2/keys/\", s.handleB2KeyDelete)     // DELETE=Delete by ID\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/metrics\", s.metrics.Handler())\n\n\t// Dashboard routes\n\tif s.dashboard != nil {\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard\", s.dashboard.Handler())\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/\", s.dashboard.Handler()) // For prefix navigation\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/object\", s.dashboard.ObjectDetailHandler())\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/metrics\", s.dashboard.MetricsHandler())\n\n\t\t// Key rotation proxy handler\n\t\tadminClient := &http.Client{\n\t\t\tTimeout: 30 * time.Minute, // Key rotation can take a long time\n\t\t}\n\t\tadminURL := \"http://\" + s.config.AdminListen + \"/admin/key/rotate\"\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/admin/key/rotate\", s.dashboard.KeyRotateHandler(adminClient, adminURL))\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/admin/key/status\", s.dashboard.KeyRotateStatusHandler())\n\t}\n\n\treturn mux\n}\n\n// healthz returns the health status.\n// This is the liveness probe — it only checks that the process is alive.\n// Backend connectivity is checked by /readyz (the readiness probe).\nfunc (s *Server) healthz(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tw.Write([]byte(\"OK\"))\n}\n\n// readyz returns the readiness status.\n// When the canary monitor is running and not disabled, its in-memory health\n// state is the sole signal — no backend call is made. When the canary is\n// disabled (ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true), /readyz always returns 200 and the\n// liveness probe (/healthz) is the sole health guard. When the canary is not\n// configured, the manifest writer's last flush is used as the health signal.\nfunc (s *Server) readyz(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t// When canary is explicitly disabled, skip all backend checks.\n\tif s.canaryDisabled {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Canary monitor is authoritative when running.\n\tif s.canary != nil && s.canaryStarted {\n\t\tif !s.canary.IsHealthy() {\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - canary check failed\"))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Fallback: manifest writer's last successful delta flush.\n\t// A flush within the last 60 seconds indicates the service is healthy.\n\tconst flushThreshold = 60 * time.Second\n\tif s.manifestWriter != nil {\n\t\tlastFlush := s.manifestWriter.LastFlush()\n\t\tif !lastFlush.IsZero() && time.Since(lastFlush) < flushThreshold {\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t// No recent flush — report unhealthy\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\t\tif lastFlush.IsZero() {\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - manifest writer has never flushed\"))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(fmt.Sprintf(\"Not ready - manifest writer last flush %v ago (threshold %v)\", time.Since(lastFlush).Round(time.Second), flushThreshold)))\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Neither canary nor manifest writer available — report unhealthy.\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - no health signal available\"))\n}\n\n// verifyKey verifies the MEK is correct.\nfunc (s *Server) verifyKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif s.canary == nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unknown\",\"error\":\"canary monitor not configured\"}`))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tstatus := s.canary.GetStatus()\n\tif status.DecryptVerified && status.HMACVerified {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"verified\",\"message\":\"MEK is correct\"}`))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unverified\",\"error\":\"canary check failed - MEK may be incorrect\"}`))\n}\n\n// rotateKey rotates the MEK.\nfunc (s *Server) rotateKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Read the new MEK from the request body\n\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer r.Body.Close()\n\n\t// The new MEK should be a 32-byte hex-encoded string (64 hex chars)\n\t// or raw 32 bytes\n\tvar newMEK []byte\n\tif len(body) == 64 {\n\t\t// Hex-encoded\n\t\tnewMEK, err = hex.DecodeString(string(body))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid hex-encoded MEK\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t} else if len(body) == 32 {\n\t\t// Raw bytes\n\t\tnewMEK = body\n\t} else {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid MEK length: expected 32 bytes or 64 hex chars, got %d\", len(body)), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Create key rotator with the default key. Pass the manifest index so\n\t// rotateObject can skip per-object HeadObject calls when the entry is cached.\n\tdefaultKey := s.keyManager.DefaultKey()\n\trotator := NewKeyRotator(s.backend, s.config.Bucket, defaultKey.MEK, newMEK, s.manifest)\n\n\t// Perform rotation\n\tresult, err := rotator.Rotate(r.Context())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"status\":  \"failed\",\n\t\t\t\"error\":   err.Error(),\n\t\t\t\"result\":  result,\n\t\t})\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Update the server's MEK on success\n\tif result.Status == \"completed\" {\n\t\tif err := s.keyManager.UpdateDefaultKey(newMEK); err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"error\": err.Error(),\n\t\t\t}).Error(\"failed to update key manager after rotation\")\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Clear the metadata cache since DEKs are now wrapped with new MEK\n\t\ts.cache.Clear()\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(result)\n}\n\n// exportKey exports the current MEK.\nfunc (s *Server) exportKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif r.URL.Query().Get(\"confirm\") != \"yes\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Must include ?confirm=yes to export key\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Export the default MEK as hex-encoded string\n\tdefaultKey := s.keyManager.DefaultKey()\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]string{\n\t\t\"mek\":   hex.EncodeToString(defaultKey.MEK),\n\t\t\"format\": \"hex\",\n\t\t\"warning\": \"This key provides access to all encrypted data. Store securely.\",\n\t})\n}\n\n// canaryHandler returns the canary status.\nfunc (s *Server) canaryHandler(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif s.canary == nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unknown\",\"error\":\"canary monitor not configured\"}`))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tstatus := s.canary.GetStatus()\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(status)\n}\n\n// audit returns the audit status.\nfunc (s *Server) audit(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Create auditor and perform audit\n\tauditor := provenance.NewAuditor(s.backend, s.config.Bucket)\n\tresult, err := auditor.Audit(r.Context())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"status\": \"error\",\n\t\t\t\"error\":   err.Error(),\n\t\t})\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(result)\n}\n\n// wrapHandler wraps a handler with common middleware.\nfunc (s *Server) wrapHandler(h http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\t\t// Track in-flight request\n\t\ts.requestTracker.Start()\n\t\tdefer s.requestTracker.End()\n\n\t\t// Log request\n\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"method\": r.Method,\n\t\t\t\"path\":   r.URL.Path,\n\t\t}).Debug(\"incoming request\")\n\n\t\t// Add CORS headers for browser clients\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Access-Control-Allow-Origin\", \"*\")\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Access-Control-Allow-Methods\", \"GET, PUT, DELETE, HEAD, POST, OPTIONS\")\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Access-Control-Allow-Headers\", \"Authorization, Content-Type, Range, Content-Length\")\n\n\t\t// Handle preflight\n\t\tif r.Method == http.MethodOptions {\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify auth for non-public endpoints\n\t\tif !s.isPublicPath(r.URL.Path) {\n\t\t\tcred, err := s.verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Invalid credentials\", 403)\n\t\t\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(\"auth\", 403)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Check ACL for the request. For list operations the URL path has no\n\t\t\t// key component, so fall back to the ?prefix query param so that ACL\n\t\t\t// prefix restrictions are enforced correctly against the listed prefix.\n\t\t\tbucket, key := s.extractBucketAndKey(r)\n\t\t\tif key == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tkey = r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif err := CheckACL(cred, bucket, key); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Access Denied\", 403)\n\t\t\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(\"acl\", 403)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Use a response writer wrapper to capture status code\n\t\trw := &responseWriter{ResponseWriter: w, statusCode: http.StatusOK}\n\n\t\th(rw, r)\n\n\t\t// Record metrics\n\t\tduration := time.Since(start)\n\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(r.Method, rw.statusCode)\n\t\ts.metrics.RecordRequestDuration(r.Method, duration)\n\n\t\t// Log completed request\n\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"method\":      r.Method,\n\t\t\t\"path\":        r.URL.Path,\n\t\t\t\"status\":      rw.statusCode,\n\t\t\t\"duration_ms\": duration.Milliseconds(),\n\t\t}).Info(\"request completed\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// responseWriter wraps http.ResponseWriter to capture the status code.\ntype responseWriter struct {\n\thttp.ResponseWriter\n\tstatusCode int\n}\n\n// WriteHeader captures the status code.\nfunc (rw *responseWriter) WriteHeader(code int) {\n\trw.statusCode = code\n\trw.ResponseWriter.WriteHeader(code)\n}\n\n// isPublicPath checks if a path is public (no auth required).\nfunc (s *Server) isPublicPath(path string) bool {\n\treturn path == \"/healthz\" || path == \"/readyz\"\n}\n\n// verifyAuthAndGetCredential validates AWS SigV4 authentication and returns the credential.\nfunc (s *Server) verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r *http.Request) (*config.Credential, error) {\n\t// Create auth with all credentials\n\tauth := NewSigV4AuthWithCredentials(s.config.Credentials, s.config.B2Region)\n\n\t// Check for query-based auth (presigned URLs)\n\tif r.URL.Query().Get(\"X-Amz-Credential\") != \"\" {\n\t\treturn auth.VerifyQueryAuth(r)\n\t}\n\n\t// Check for header-based auth\n\tauthHeader := r.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")\n\tif authHeader == \"\" {\n\t\treturn nil, ErrMissingAuthHeader\n\t}\n\n\t// Pass nil body — buildCanonicalRequest uses x-amz-content-sha256 header\n\t// when present (which covers all AWS SDK/CLI requests), falling back to\n\t// sha256(body) for requests without that header.\n\treturn auth.VerifyRequest(r, nil)\n}\n\n// extractBucketAndKey extracts bucket and key from the request URL.\nfunc (s *Server) extractBucketAndKey(r *http.Request) (bucket, key string) {\n\tpath := r.URL.Path\n\t// Remove leading slash\n\tpath = strings.TrimPrefix(path, \"/\")\n\n\t// Check for virtual-hosted-style (bucket in host)\n\t// For path-style: /bucket/key\n\tparts := strings.SplitN(path, \"/\", 2)\n\tif len(parts) >= 1 {\n\t\tbucket = parts[0]\n\t}\n\tif len(parts) >= 2 {\n\t\tkey = parts[1]\n\t\t// URL decode the key (DuckDB httpfs encodes special chars like = as %3D)\n\t\tif decoded, err := url.PathUnescape(key); err == nil {\n\t\t\tkey = decoded\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Use configured bucket if empty\n\tif bucket == \"\" {\n\t\tbucket = s.config.Bucket\n\t}\n\n\treturn bucket, key\n}\n\n// writeError writes an S3 error response.\nfunc (s *Server) writeError(w http.ResponseWriter, code, message string, statusCode int) {\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/xml\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(statusCode)\n\tvar codeBuf, msgBuf bytes.Buffer\n\txml.EscapeText(&codeBuf, []byte(code))\n\txml.EscapeText(&msgBuf, []byte(message))\n\tfmt.Fprintf(w, `<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>`+\"\\n<Error>\\n  <Code>%s</Code>\\n  <Message>%s</Message>\\n</Error>\",\n\t\tcodeBuf.String(), msgBuf.String())\n}\n\n// GenerateDEK generates a new DEK (exposed for handlers).\nfunc (s *Server) GenerateDEK() ([]byte, error) {\n\treturn crypto.GenerateDEK()\n}\n\n// GenerateIV generates a new IV (exposed for handlers).\nfunc (s *Server) GenerateIV() ([]byte, error) {\n\treturn crypto.GenerateIV()\n}\n\n// WaitForInFlightRequests waits for all in-flight requests to complete.\nfunc (s *Server) WaitForInFlightRequests() {\n\ts.requestTracker.Wait()\n}\n\n// InFlightRequestCount returns the current number of in-flight requests.\nfunc (s *Server) InFlightRequestCount() int64 {\n\treturn s.requestTracker.Count()\n}\n\n// handlePresign generates a pre-signed URL for sharing encrypted files.\n// POST /admin/presign\n// Body: {\"bucket\": \"my-bucket\", \"key\": \"path/to/file.parquet\", \"expires_in\": \"1h\", \"content_disposition\": \"attachment; filename=\\\"file.parquet\\\"\"}\nfunc (s *Server) handlePresign(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify auth\n\tcred, err := s.verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Invalid credentials\", 403)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse request body\n\tvar req struct {\n\t\tBucket             string `json:\"bucket\"`\n\t\tKey                string `json:\"key\"`\n\t\tExpiresIn          string `json:\"expires_in\"`\n\t\tContentDisposition string `json:\"content_disposition\"`\n\t\tRange              string `json:\"range\"`\n\t}\n\n\tif err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Use configured bucket if not specified\n\tbucket := req.Bucket\n\tif bucket == \"\" {\n\t\tbucket = s.config.Bucket\n\t}\n\n\t// Validate required fields\n\tif req.Key == \"\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"key is required\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check ACL for the request\n\tif err := CheckACL(cred, bucket, req.Key); err != nil {\n\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Access Denied\", 403)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse expiration (default 1 hour)\n\texpiration := presign.DefaultExpiration\n\tif req.ExpiresIn != \"\" {\n\t\texpiration, err = presign.ParseExpiration(req.ExpiresIn)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid expires_in: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Build options\n\tvar opts []presign.Option\n\tif req.ContentDisposition != \"\" {\n\t\topts = append(opts, presign.WithContentDisposition(req.ContentDisposition))\n\t}\n\tif req.Range != \"\" {\n\t\topts = append(opts, presign.WithRange(req.Range))\n\t}\n\n\t// Generate pre-signed URL\n\tshareURL, err := s.presigner.GenerateURL(bucket, req.Key, expiration, opts...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate URL: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Return response\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"url\":       shareURL,\n\t\t\"expires_in\": presign.FormatExpiration(expiration),\n\t\t\"expires_at\": time.Now().Add(expiration).UTC().Format(time.RFC3339),\n\t})\n}\n\n// handleShare serves decrypted content from a pre-signed URL token.\n// GET /share/<token>\nfunc (s *Server) handleShare(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Extract token from path\n\ttokenStr := presign.ParseTokenFromPath(r.URL.Path)\n\tif tokenStr == \"\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Missing token\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify token\n\ttoken, err := s.presigner.VerifyToken(tokenStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, presign.ErrExpiredToken) {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Link expired\", http.StatusGone)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, presign.ErrInvalidSignature) {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid link\", http.StatusForbidden)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid token\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Get object metadata\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tinfo, err := s.backend.Head(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Object not found: %v\", err), http.StatusNotFound)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if object is ARMOR-encrypted\n\tif !info.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t// Serve non-ARMOR objects directly (passthrough)\n\t\tbody, _, err := s.backend.Get(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to get object: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer body.Close()\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Length\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", info.Size))\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", info.ContentType)\n\t\tif token.ContentDisposition != \"\" {\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Disposition\", token.ContentDisposition)\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tio.Copy(w, body)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse ARMOR metadata\n\tarmorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(info.Metadata)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to parse object metadata\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Get the MEK for this object\n\tmek, err := s.keyManager.GetMEKByID(armorMeta.KeyID)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to get decryption key\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Unwrap DEK\n\tdek, err := crypto.UnwrapDEK(mek, armorMeta.WrappedDEK)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to unwrap DEK\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Create decryptor\n\tdecryptor, err := crypto.NewDecryptor(dek, armorMeta.IV, armorMeta.BlockSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to create decryptor\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Set response headers\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Length\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", armorMeta.PlaintextSize))\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", armorMeta.ContentType)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Accept-Ranges\", \"bytes\")\n\tif token.ContentDisposition != \"\" {\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Disposition\", token.ContentDisposition)\n\t}\n\n\t// Handle range request if specified in token or header\n\trangeHeader := token.Range\n\tif rangeHeader == \"\" {\n\t\trangeHeader = r.Header.Get(\"Range\")\n\t}\n\n\tif rangeHeader != \"\" {\n\t\ts.handleShareRangeRequest(w, r, token, decryptor, armorMeta, rangeHeader)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Full object download\n\ts.handleShareFullObject(w, r, token, decryptor, armorMeta)\n}\n\n// handleShareFullObject handles full object downloads for share endpoint.\nfunc (s *Server) handleShareFullObject(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, token *presign.Token, decryptor *crypto.Decryptor, armorMeta *backend.ARMORMetadata) {\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\n\tblockSize := armorMeta.BlockSize\n\tblockCount := int(crypto.ComputeBlockCount(armorMeta.PlaintextSize, blockSize))\n\tplaintextSize := armorMeta.PlaintextSize\n\n\t// Calculate offsets\n\thmacTableOffset := crypto.HeaderSize + plaintextSize\n\thmacTableSize := int64(blockCount) * crypto.HMACSize\n\n\t// 1. Prefetch HMAC table\n\thmacBody, err := s.backend.GetRange(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key, hmacTableOffset, hmacTableSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to fetch HMAC table: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\thmacTable, err := io.ReadAll(hmacBody)\n\thmacBody.Close()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read HMAC table: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// 2. Stream data from Cloudflare\n\tstreamSize := crypto.HeaderSize + plaintextSize\n\tdataBody, err := s.backend.GetRange(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key, 0, streamSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to get object stream: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer dataBody.Close()\n\n\t// 3. Read and discard header\n\theaderBuf := make([]byte, crypto.HeaderSize)\n\tif _, err := io.ReadFull(dataBody, headerBuf); err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read header: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// 4. Write status before streaming\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\n\t// 5. Stream decrypt\n\tencryptedBuf := make([]byte, blockSize)\n\tfor blockIndex := 0; blockIndex < blockCount; blockIndex++ {\n\t\tremaining := plaintextSize - int64(blockIndex)*int64(blockSize)\n\t\tactualBlockSize := int(min64(int64(blockSize), remaining))\n\n\t\tencryptedBuf = encryptedBuf[:actualBlockSize]\n\t\tn, err := io.ReadFull(dataBody, encryptedBuf)\n\t\tif err != nil && err != io.EOF && err != io.ErrUnexpectedEOF {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif n == 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tencryptedBuf = encryptedBuf[:n]\n\n\t\t// Verify HMAC\n\t\thmacOffset := blockIndex * crypto.HMACSize\n\t\tif hmacOffset+crypto.HMACSize > len(hmacTable) {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\texpectedHMAC := hmacTable[hmacOffset : hmacOffset+crypto.HMACSize]\n\n\t\tmac := hmac.New(sha256.New, decryptor.HMACKey())\n\t\tindexBytes := make([]byte, 4)\n\t\tbinary.BigEndian.PutUint32(indexBytes, uint32(blockIndex))\n\t\tmac.Write(indexBytes)\n\t\tmac.Write(encryptedBuf)\n\t\tcomputed := mac.Sum(nil)\n\n\t\tif !hmac.Equal(computed, expectedHMAC) {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Decrypt\n\t\tdecrypted := make([]byte, n)\n\t\tctr := makeCounter(armorMeta.IV, uint32(blockIndex))\n\t\tstream := cipher.NewCTR(decryptor.CipherBlock(), ctr)\n\t\tstream.XORKeyStream(decrypted, encryptedBuf)\n\n\t\t// Write to client\n\t\tw.Write(decrypted)\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleShareRangeRequest handles range requests for share endpoint.\nfunc (s *Server) handleShareRangeRequest(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, token *presign.Token, decryptor *crypto.Decryptor, armorMeta *backend.ARMORMetadata, rangeHeader string) {\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tplaintextSize := armorMeta.PlaintextSize\n\n\t// Parse range header\n\tstart, end, err := parseRangeHeader(rangeHeader, plaintextSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid range\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Translate range to encrypted blocks\n\ttranslation, err := crypto.TranslateRange(start, end, plaintextSize, armorMeta.BlockSize, crypto.HeaderSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to translate range: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Fetch encrypted blocks and HMAC table in parallel\n\tvar encrypted, hmacTable []byte\n\n\tg, gctx := errgroup.WithContext(ctx)\n\n\tg.Go(func() error {\n\t\tencryptedBody, err := s.backend.GetRange(gctx, token.Bucket, token.Key, translation.DataOffset, translation.DataLength)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to fetch encrypted blocks: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer encryptedBody.Close()\n\n\t\tencrypted, err = io.ReadAll(encryptedBody)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to read encrypted blocks: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t})\n\n\tg.Go(func() error {\n\t\thmacBody, err := s.backend.GetRange(gctx, token.Bucket, token.Key, translation.HMACOffset, translation.HMACLength)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to fetch HMAC table: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer hmacBody.Close()\n\n\t\thmacTable, err = io.ReadAll(hmacBody)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to read HMAC table: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t})\n\n\tif err := g.Wait(); err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Decrypt range\n\tplaintext, err := decryptor.DecryptRange(encrypted, hmacTable, start, end, plaintextSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to decrypt range: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Set response headers\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Length\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", len(plaintext)))\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Range\", fmt.Sprintf(\"bytes %d-%d/%d\", start, end, plaintextSize))\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusPartialContent)\n\tw.Write(plaintext)\n}\n\nfunc min64(a, b int64) int64 {\n\tif a < b {\n\t\treturn a\n\t}\n\treturn b\n}\n\n// makeCounter creates a 16-byte counter value from the IV and block index.\nfunc makeCounter(iv []byte, blockIndex uint32) []byte {\n\tcounter := make([]byte, 16)\n\tcopy(counter[0:12], iv[0:12])\n\tbinary.BigEndian.PutUint32(counter[12:16], blockIndex)\n\treturn counter\n}\n\n// parseRangeHeader parses a Range header like \"bytes=0-1023\".\nfunc parseRangeHeader(header string, totalSize int64) (start, end int64, err error) {\n\tif !strings.HasPrefix(header, \"bytes=\") {\n\t\treturn 0, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid range format\")\n\t}\n\n\trangeSpec := strings.TrimPrefix(header, \"bytes=\")\n\n\tif strings.Contains(rangeSpec, \",\") {\n\t\treturn 0, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"multiple ranges not supported\")\n\t}\n\n\tparts := strings.Split(rangeSpec, \"-\")\n\tif len(parts) != 2 {\n\t\treturn 0, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid range format\")\n\t}\n\n\tif parts[0] == \"\" {\n\t\t// Suffix range: -500 means last 500 bytes\n\t\tsuffix, err := strconv.ParseInt(parts[1], 10, 64)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn 0, 0, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tstart = totalSize - suffix\n\t\tend = totalSize - 1\n\t} else {\n\t\tstart, err = strconv.ParseInt(parts[0], 10, 64)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn 0, 0, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parts[1] == \"\" {\n\t\t\tend = totalSize - 1\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tend, err = strconv.ParseInt(parts[1], 10, 64)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, 0, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif start < 0 || start >= totalSize || end < start || end >= totalSize {\n\t\treturn 0, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"range out of bounds\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn start, end, nil\n}\n\n// handleB2Keys handles B2 application key management.\n// GET: List keys\n// POST: Create a new key\nfunc (s *Server) handleB2Keys(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif s.b2keys == nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, `{\"error\":\"B2 key management not available - check B2 credentials\"}`, http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tswitch r.Method {\n\tcase http.MethodGet:\n\t\ts.listB2Keys(w, r)\n\tcase http.MethodPost:\n\t\ts.createB2Key(w, r)\n\tdefault:\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t}\n}\n\n// listB2Keys lists B2 application keys.\nfunc (s *Server) listB2Keys(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tcount := 100\n\tif c := r.URL.Query().Get(\"count\"); c != \"\" {\n\t\tif parsed, err := strconv.Atoi(c); err == nil && parsed > 0 {\n\t\t\tcount = parsed\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tcursor := r.URL.Query().Get(\"cursor\")\n\n\tresult, err := s.b2keys.ListKeys(r.Context(), count, cursor)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"error\": err.Error(),\n\t\t}).Error(\"Failed to list B2 keys\")\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(`{\"error\":\"Failed to list keys: %v\"}`, err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(result)\n}\n\n// createB2Key creates a new B2 application key.\nfunc (s *Server) createB2Key(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tvar req b2keys.CreateKeyRequest\n\tif err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(`{\"error\":\"Invalid request body: %v\"}`, err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif req.Name == \"\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, `{\"error\":\"name is required\"}`, http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif len(req.Capabilities) == 0 {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, `{\"error\":\"capabilities is required\"}`, http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tkey, err := s.b2keys.CreateKey(r.Context(), &req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"error\": err.Error(),\n\t\t\t\"name\":  req.Name,\n\t\t}).Error(\"Failed to create B2 key\")\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(`{\"error\":\"Failed to create key: %v\"}`, err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"key_id\": key.ID,\n\t\t\"name\":   key.Name,\n\t}).Info(\"Created B2 application key\")\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusCreated)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(key)\n}\n\n// handleB2KeyDelete handles DELETE /admin/b2/keys/{id}.\nfunc (s *Server) handleB2KeyDelete(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif s.b2keys == nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, `{\"error\":\"B2 key management not available - check B2 credentials\"}`, http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodDelete {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\",
